posted:Posted May 9, 2024
msg:Environment: It was my first time in Suining, and I was very impressed. I can say that the food was good and the environment was good, but the air was really not good.

Facilities: I was very impressed with this hotel. It was a long way from the parking lot to the front desk and then to the room. I changed elevators in the middle and walked through the huge lobby.

Service: The restaurant hardware is of five-star standard, but many details of decoration and construction technology are still not up to standard, but it is top-notch for a city of this level. The breakfast food is also delicious.
The parking path was a bit confusing when we arrived. We went around and reversed on the ramp at the hotel entrance before we found the parking lot entrance. (Of course, we reversed under the guidance of the staff) But the strange thing is that when I missed the turn and hesitated to find the way, no staff member showed the way. Three men in work clothes were chatting with all their heart. None of them were in working condition. I hope to improve training.
The good hotels in Suining are all in this area, very close and concentrated.
